unsigned int invert(int x, int p, int n)
{
  unsigned int mask = ~(~0 << n) << (p - n + 1);

  return x ^ mask;
}

// Function to invert n bits starting from position p in x
unsigned int invert(int x, int p, int n)
{
  return x ^ (~(~0 << n) << (p - n + 1));
}
